                        <div data-reactid="676">
                         <li data-reactid="677"><p data-reactid="678">Wu was a great host! Her and her family were very warm and welcoming. </p><span data-reactid="679">Katie</span><span data-reactid="680">2016-07-26T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="681"><p data-reactid="682">Wu has a great house in Torrance. I used to live a few blocks from here and the neighborhood is nice and walkable. Ralphs, dry cleaning, post office, pharmacy all in a short walk. The BnB space is large, a bit like a loft. You get the private entrance and a big front window with plenty of light. The kitchen and bathroom are both large, and the shower is particularly nice! Comfy bed, fast wifi. My arrival was smooth, Wu is very communicative and while at work arranged for her lovely family to show me in and hand over the key. The apartment has such great potential and with some minor adjustments it would really put it to another level. So, here are my humble suggestions: The kitchen is not yet so useful as it is not stocked with any utensils, pots, pans, plates etc. When traveling this makes it a bit ornamental. The fridge was unplugged and at room temp, so that cramped my ability to store food for the first day. Might need a little clean too in there, but no big deal. The bathroom could use a little tidy up - just minor stuff like water/soap spots on mirrors, taps, counter. The shower is really great but the drain is partly clogged. Within about 30 seconds there is standing water, so that should probably get sorted soon. In conclusion, it's a great spot, great value, just needs little tweaks to make it perfect! Thanks so much for sharing your home Wu!</p><span data-reactid="683">Dan</span><span data-reactid="684">2016-07-16T00:00:00Z</span></li>
